(the &#8220;Company&#8221; or &#8220;Spirit&#8221;) issued a press release announcing its unaudited financial results for the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">second</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;quarter </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">2015</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">; a copy of which is attached hereto as Exhibit 99.1 and is incorporated herein by reference.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;text-indent:48px;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"></font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">Non-GAAP financial measures that reflect adjustments from historical financial data prepared under GAAP, including adjustments for special items, are included in the press release as supplemental disclosures because the Company believes they are useful indicators of the Company's operating performance for comparative purposes.  These non-GAAP financial measures are well recognized performance measurements in the airline industry that are frequently used by investors, securities analysts and other interested parties in comparing the operating performance of companies in the airline industry.  The non-GAAP financial measures provided have limitations as an analytical tool.  Because of these limitations determinations of our operating performance adjusted for special items should not be considered in isolation or as a substitute for performance measures calculated in accordance with GAAP.  The Company has also provided in the press release reconciliations of these non-GAAP financial measures to the appropriate GAAP financial measures.</font></div><div GAAP net income for the </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">second</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">&#32;quarter </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:none;">2015</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">&#32;increased </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">18.3</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">&#32;percent year over year to </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:none;">$76.7 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">&#32;(</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:none;">$1.05</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">&#32;per diluted share). </font></div></td></tr></table><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;padding-left:48px;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt;"><tr><td style="width:48px;"></td><td></td></tr><tr><td style="vertical-align:top"><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:11pt;padding-left:24px;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">&#8226;</font></div></td><td style="vertical-align:top;"><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">Adjusted pre-tax margin for the </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">second</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">&#32;quarter </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:none;">2015</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">&#32;was </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">21.3 percent</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;"><sup style="vertical-align:top;line-height:120%;font-size:7pt">1</sup></font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">.  On a GAAP basis, pre-tax margin for the </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">second</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">&#32;quarter </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:none;">2015</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">&#32;was </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">21.8 percent</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">.  </font></div></td></tr></table><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt;"><tr><td style="width:48px;"></td><td></td></tr><tr><td style="vertical-align:top"><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:11pt;padding-left:24px;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">&#8226;</font></div></td><td style="vertical-align:top;"><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">Spirit ended the </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">second</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">quarter</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">&#32;2015 with unrestricted cash and cash equivalents of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:none;">$769.3 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">. </font></div></td></tr></table><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt;"><tr><td style="width:48px;"></td><td></td></tr><tr><td style="vertical-align:top"><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:11pt;padding-left:24px;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">&#8226;</font></div></td><td style="vertical-align:top;"><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">Spirit's return on invested capital (before taxes and excluding special items) for the twelve months ended </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:none;">June&#160;30, 2015</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">&#32;was </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">29.4 percent</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;"><sup style="vertical-align:top;line-height:120%;font-size:7pt">2</sup></font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">.  </font></div></td></tr></table><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">"Our second quarter 2015 performance was negatively impacted by an unusual number of storms and I want to thank our team members and business partners for their hard work and dedication in serving our customers and helping us to restore our operations to normal," said Ben Baldanza, Spirit&#8217;s Chief Executive Officer.  "In addition to an unusual number of storms, we&#8217;ve recently seen a noticeable change in competitive pricing behavior. But, the fundamentals of our business haven&#8217;t changed:&#160; we continue to grow our network while maintaining high margins, delivering strong returns, and offering our customers low fares."</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">During June, Spirit experienced consecutive storm systems in Dallas, Chicago, New York, and Detroit followed by Tropical Storm Bill that sat over Houston before moving north to Dallas. The timing and location of these storm systems produced a domino effect on the Company's operation resulting in over 500 flight cancellations and numerous flight delays. Due to the sheer volume of flights affected, the Company was unable to flex up staffing levels enough to mitigate the impact of crews being displaced or being unable to work due to them reaching their contractual or regulatory work hour maximums. These challenges lengthened the span of the irregular operation and the time it took to restore the system to normal.  With its high aircraft utilization, low daily flight frequency and point-to-point network, severe irregular operations typically create a unique set of challenges for the Company; however, the Company believes the unusual number and location of storms in June exacerbated the operational difficulty and made this event unlike others.  The Company estimates the impact of the cancellations, delays, and other non-recurring expenses during the quarter negatively impacted operating income by $20 million ($5 million lower revenue, $15 million higher costs).   Adjusting for these items, the Company estimates it would have reported adjusted net income of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">$87.5 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">&#32;(</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">$1.20</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">&#32;per diluted share).</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;font-style:italic;">Revenue Performance </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">&#32;</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">For the </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:none;">second</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">&#32;quarter </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:none;">2015</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">, Spirit's total operating revenue was </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:none;">$553.4 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">, an </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:none;">increase</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">&#32;of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:none;">10.8</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">&#32;percent compared to the </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:none;">second</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">&#32;quarter </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:none;">2014</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">, driven by an increase in flight volume, partially offset by a decrease in operating yields.</font></div><br><div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">1</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><a name="sA738BA1ACD7C2F96429E6C9D285542E6"></a><div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div><br><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">Total revenue per passenger flight segment ("PFS") for the </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:none;">second</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">&#32;quarter </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:none;">2015</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:none;">decreased</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:none;">12.4 percent</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">&#32;year over year to </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:none;">$122.59</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">, primarily driven by a </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">19.4 percent</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">&#32;decrease in ticket revenue per PFS.  The decline in ticket revenue per PFS was driven by lower fare levels as a result of increased competitive pressures as well as a higher percentage of the Company&#8217;s markets being under development compared to the same period last year.  Although slightly lower year over year on a per PFS basis, non-ticket revenue continues to provide a stable revenue stream that is increasingly important during periods of lower passenger yields.  Non-ticket revenue per PFS only declined </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">1.7 percent</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">&#32;year over year to </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">$54.24</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">. The decrease in non-ticket revenue per PFS was primarily attributable to lower bag revenue per PFS and the outsourcing of the Company's onboard catering to a third-party provider under a revenue share agreement.  </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">Total revenue per available seat mile (&#8220;RASM&#8221;) for the </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">second</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">&#32;quarter </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">2015</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">decreased</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">14.8</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">&#32;percent  compared to the </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">second</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">&#32;quarter </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">2014</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">&#32;on a capacity increase of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">30.1 percent</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">.  The RASM decrease was driven by lower fare levels as a result of increased competitive pressures as well as the ramp up growth in the Company's new and mature markets.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;font-style:italic;">Cost Performance</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">Total operating expenses for the </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">second</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">&#32;quarter </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:none;">2015</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">, excluding </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">$2.9 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">&#32;of credits related to special items, increased </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">10.4 percent</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">to </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">$434.0 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;"><sup style="vertical-align:top;line-height:120%;font-size:7pt">3</sup></font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">.  Including special items, total operating expenses increased </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:none;">9.4</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">&#32;percent year over year to </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:none;">$431.1 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">.  Operating expenses benefited from economic fuel expense decreasing </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">14.8</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">&#32;percent, or </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">$22.8 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">, on a fuel volume increase of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">27.8</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">&#32;percent. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">&#160;</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">Spirit reported </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">second</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">&#32;quarter </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:none;">2015</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">&#32;cost per available seat mile ("ASM") excluding special items and fuel (&#8220;Adjusted CASM ex-fuel&#8221;)</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;"><sup style="vertical-align:top;line-height:120%;font-size:7pt">3</sup></font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">&#32;of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:none;">5.80 cent</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">s, </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">a decrease</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">&#32;of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:none;">2.5 percent</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">&#32;compared to the same period last year, driven primarily by lower aircraft rent per ASM, lower distribution expense per ASM, and lower labor expense per ASM.  These benefits were partially offset by higher passenger re-accommodation expense per ASM.  The decrease in aircraft rent per ASM was driven by a change in the mix of leased (rent recorded under aircraft rent) and purchased (depreciation recorded under depreciation and amortization) aircraft.  Lower distribution expense per ASM was in part driven by lower credit card rates related to the modification and extension of Spirit's credit card processor agreement in late 2014.  Labor expense per ASM in the second quarter 2015 was lower compared to the same period last year primarily due to scale benefits from overall growth and from larger gauge aircraft, partially offset by higher health care costs.  Passenger re-accommodation expense (recorded under other operating expense) per ASM was primarily higher year over year due to the impact from an unusual number of storm systems that disrupted the Company's operations.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">"Due to the financial impact of the unusual number of cancellations, delays, and other non-recurring items during the quarter, as well as higher healthcare costs, we have revised our full year 2015 Adjusted CASM ex-fuel range and now estimate it will be down 5 to 6 percent year over year,&#8221; said Ted Christie, Spirit's Chief Financial Officer.  "Despite these adjustments, I am encouraged about how the business is performing, which establishes a solid base for improved cost performance in 2016 and beyond." </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;font-style:italic;">Share Repurchase </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">Spirit repurchased approximately 1 million shares during the second quarter, which equated to approximately $67.5 million of the total $100 million authorization.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;font-style:italic;">Fleet</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">In the </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">second</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">&#32;quarter </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:none;">2015</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">, Spirit took delivery of 3 new A320 aircraft, ending the </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">quarter</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">&#32;with </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:none;">73</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#595959;">&#32;aircraft in its fleet.&#160; Our customers start with an unbundled, stripped-down Bare Fare&#8482; and get Frill Control&#8482; which allows them to pay only for the options they choose - like bags, seat assignments and refreshments - the things other airlines bake right into their ticket prices. We help people save money and travel more often, create new jobs and stimulate business growth in the communities we serve. With our modern and fuel-efficient all-Airbus fleet, we operate more than 360 daily flights to 57 destinations in the U.S., Latin America and the Caribbean. style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div><br><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:13px;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">The Company believes economic fuel expense is the best measure of the effect fuel prices are currently having on our business, because it most closely approximates the net cash outflow associated with purchasing fuel used for our operations during the period. Economic fuel expense is defined as into-plane fuel expense, realized gains or losses on derivative contracts, plus the economic premium expense related to fuel option contracts in the period the option is benefiting. The key difference between aircraft fuel expense as recorded in our statement of operations and economic fuel expense is unrealized mark-to-market changes in the value of aircraft fuel derivatives outstanding and the timing of premium gain or loss recognition on our outstanding fuel option contracts.&#160;Many industry analysts evaluate airline results using economic fuel expense, and it is used in our internal management reporting. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;font-weight:bold;">Reconciliation of
